name:R‚Äço‚Äçb‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Superior Double Room
info:Stayed in July 2022
info:Solo travelers
info:6 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted August 7, 2022
msg:Situated at the rear of a modern, air-conditioned shopping centre, this hotel is very well located for a range of activities.

It has a fantastic outdoor pool, hugely popular with families. The views from the pool look out across the sea. Nearby is a pool area bar and sun loungers.

The hotel has mumerous redtaurants to suit tastes and high spenders but there is a missed opportunity for a coffee shop where simple, quick sandwich type snacks could be quickly obtained.

The hotel shop was conveniently stocked....no worries for those running out of coffee, toiletries, beach/pool essentials. Open til 10pm and priced comparative to local businesses.

Reception staff are extremely helpful, friendly and will go out of their way to assist. They have the all important local knowledge, so don't be worried about where to go for testing etc, they can direct you nicely. For pandemic controls there are 2 close-by:  one in the local park, it is free, operates 9 to 12 and 3 to 6; the hospital one operates 9 to 6, has less queuing time, is a longer walk and costs 15¬•.

Pandemic measures at the hotel were excellent, showing proof of 24/48 covid testing on the local app.

Security at night, Bell Boys during the day, always on hand to assist.

Didi taxis pull up in front of the hotel.

Rooms either view the sea or the hillside. These rooms have ensuite shower and toet, sink, bath and come with very comfortable beds, pitched at the right height so good orthopedics. Airconditioning in the room is higjly adjustable and very responsive.

Little fridge with soft drinks mini bar and 2 free bottles of water per day. Great to store fruits, yoghurts and milk. 

As a British traveller, I am used to holiday hotels and the Harman, as with a lot in Sanya, has no balcony. That is a miss because I often like to sut outdoors and read but, I was on 10th floor of 17 floors so I can understand the safety aspect of no balcony.

Views from this hotel are superb. 

Across from reception : 49ers cocktail bar, quiet, stocked well with liquors and the lovely staff make a great cocktail or mixer. Air conditioning and sublimated lighting make thus a cosy, intimate and quiet venue; there are 2 eating areas both selling Chinese foods, one seemed to cater more for Chinese staff, sold very cheap meals of excellent quality....well worth 25RMB to have a meal with the staff. It was nothing fancy, just basic tables and chairs in a food court style setting but the meals were top notch. I fully understand why this area was popular with locals and I highly recommend it. 

It will seem odd walking round the back of the shopping mall to get to the main road, but from the hotel, you can cut through the mall, also beautifully airconditioned. Attached to the mall is a supermarket selling all you need and more.

If you drink yellow tea (British teas), bring them with you. I failed to find even Liptons here and in China, Liptons is very common. No yellow tea anywhere, that I could locate. Hotel do provide the usual freebies but I had run out and for my 12 days, had to cold-turkey no tea. 

Local buses stop by the mall and you can get to the train station easily as well as Nanshan Buddhist  area...bus 55...takes less than an hour...costs about 11RMB.

Just a short walj from the Harman gets you to the gorgeous, quiet white sand beach and the tyrquoise sea with its gently lapping waves. Stop off at the Beachlover Bar for great views sat on the beach, food and drink as well as nightly entertainment.

The choice of the Harman will not disappoint. Great for singkes, romantic couples, families and a big favourite with children. 
----------------------------------------

msg:Harman Hotel was a good place to stay in Sanya. We stayed during covid situation but the pool and the bar remained open for the guests. It has a good view of the sea and it‚Äôs close to a mall and a convenient store where you can buy anything you might need.

The hotel offers free breakfast and they have a wide variety. Western breakfast including bacon and toasts and some omelet; Asian breakfast like rice and noodles. You can try different things every day. 

The hotel had the gym and some spa/massage as well but I didnt get the chance to use it. Our room was spacious. It had the balcony with the sea view. Although it was a bit odd that the bath tub was somehow outside the shower room, it was not so bad. 

During the covid situation, the hotel delivered our breakfast to our room and it was a lot of breakfast. I felt bad for not being able to eat all of them. The staff was nice and their service was fast. 

The hotel is about 5 mins walk to the beach. They do not have a way straight to the beach as the closest way to the beach is owned by the military. You have to go all the way to the square which is about 5 to 7 mins walk. It‚Äôs not that far really. When you reach the beach, you can just choose any spot under the palm trees and beach bum all afternoon. 

Downside: No outside food and drinks at the pool bar and they are pricey. 

Overall, once you experience higher class hotels, you will never want to downgrade. Afterall, you deserve comfort on your vacation. 

We all had a great time.

msg:I‚Äôve traveled a lot, been to many countries and many hotels, both cheap and expensive, but for the first time I decided to write a review because my experience was so bad, I want to prevent other people from ruining their vacation. I was very optimistic about my trip to Sanya, and after looking at different options decided to stay in Harman Hotel, because the promotional photos looked nice and the reviews were great, also the price seemed reasonable. Well, it turned out staying there was a huge mistake. From the moment of check in, things started looking pretty dull. The staff at the reception desk didn‚Äôt speak a word of English, which is really embarrassing, more than that, only after my suggestion they unwillingly decided to use the translation app on their phone, and did so with the most miserable look upon their faces as if I owed them money. I booked a sea view room specifically with one bed, but upon arrival I was ‚Äútold‚Äù that they only have rooms with two single beds. Once I entered the room, I felt a very unpleasant dusty smell as if I walked into a crypt. The room was clean, but everything was just so old and ragged. There were multiple stains on the walls, many surfaces were abraded. It is clear that the renovation hasn‚Äôt been done in ages. The view of the sea also wasn‚Äôt spectacular because prior to the sea, you can see dirty roofs of the local slums. The infinity pool was nice for taking photos, but wasn‚Äôt suited for swimming, because it‚Äôs basically a puddle where the water level only reaches your belly. As far as the location of the hotel goes, also nothing good. There‚Äôs a huge pineapple mall right next to it, so it‚Äôs always very noisy and crowded. Makes you feel like you‚Äôre at a flee market in a third world country. The hotel doesn‚Äôt have a private beach and the public beach is located within a 10 minute walk. The beach is very nice, but then again, it‚Äôs a public beach, so this hotel has nothing to do with it. And that‚Äôs very fortunate because I have a feeling that if that beach belonged to harman hotel, it would be majorly messed up too. The breakfast was mediocre at best, mostly Chinese dishes, and pretty poorly cooked too. Also the hotel doesn‚Äôt provide the services they claim to provide. Such as in the guide book in the room it was noted that there‚Äôs a currency exchange service available at front desk. Well, of course it turned out that it‚Äôs not available and that they have never heard of it. Also, despite leaving the ‚Äúclean the room‚Äù sign on the door in the morning, the cleaning lady only comes to clean at a time comfortable for her, usually around 3 or 4 o‚Äôclock in the afternoon. Also, after a couple of nights my legs started to itch severely, and that‚Äôs very peculiar as I haven‚Äôt seen any mosquitoes. My guess is, it might have been allergy to the laundry detergent that the hotel uses. And after reading reviews where people claim they had the same problem, I‚Äôm pretty sure it has something to do with the quality and cleanliness of the sheets. Also, I had persistent problems with Wi-Fi connection, one minute it worked, and the next minute it didn‚Äôt, and of course nothing could be done to fix it. Finally, when one evening I spotted a giant cockroach on the balcony, I decided it was time to pack up and leave. I really tried to find positive things about this hotel, but I just couldn‚Äôt, every day my impression was worse and worse, and so was my mood. I am very surprised to see so many good reviews on this one, because I wouldn‚Äôt recommend this hotel to my worst enemy. Maybe if you book the cheapest option at this hotel, it could somehow be justified (although I seriously doubt it), but if you book rooms at 800+, then definitely look at other hotels, I‚Äôm sure there are many better options for this money.

Our two-year-old child bumped into the bed in the middle of the night, and his teeth hit the edge of the bedside table, causing two teeth to be penetrated. The child cried in pain, and the mother was in pain.
2. The hotel did not take action after the accident! ! ! As a foreign tourist, I called the hotel for help as soon as possible. After a long time, the hotel sent iodine and left. . . Sanya People's Hospital did not dare to take it. The Chinese Medicine Hospital recommended going to a cooperative beauty institution. It was transferred to Haitang Bay to Haizong before the disease was cured. This incident is also the biggest pain point of our wonderful holiday.
The hotel has many advantages, but I sincerely hope that you will pay attention to safety issues, carefully place furniture, and remind children and the elderly. I hope the hotel will get better and better! Don't do good things for small things!

Based on the Food Safety Regulations: If foreign objects are found in the food, the operator may be required to pay ten times the price or three times the loss; if the amount of additional compensation is less than 1,000 yuan, the compensation shall be 1,000 yuan. Producers and operators who receive compensation claims from consumers shall implement the first responsibility system, pay compensation in advance, and shall not shirk their excuses;
I didn't ask for a claim of 1,000, because I think you can get anything if you order a takeaway in the current environment, not to mention the hotel, which I can understand. So I proposed to refund the room fee for one night (478 yuan, as compensation)
The person in charge of the hotel's catering expressed the hope of a discount of 15%. I also agree. The room facilities are quite satisfactory, the air conditioning is adequate, and there are a variety of pillows to choose from. The network TV channels are very comprehensive, and can be watched back, it is very convenient to follow the drama. Except that the TV remote control is not very sensitive due to excessive use, the room facilities are very good. There is no such thing as a "musty smell".

The breakfast buffet is very rich. The breakfast time at Harman Hotel lasts until 1:30 noon. You must order a big compliment!

The swimming pool is very large, divided into children and adults. The children's pool is bigger than the adult pool and provides a variety of water toys. The swimming pool closes at 11pm. Because the swimming pool is on the sixth floor of the hotel, you can enjoy the invincible sea view from the infinity pool.

It is recommended to book a sea view room.
